 On this seat, the Congress gave the ticket to Sawaram Patel
 chagan singh ne savaaram ko 31048 maton se haraakar jeet darj kii he
 Chhagan Singh got 74928 votes, while Savaram got 43880
 is seat par tisare number par basapa ke pankaj rahe
 He received 22808 votes
 congress kii duubati naiya ke khewanhaar bane gahalot, kya CM banenge?siton ke lihaaj se rajasthan ke sabase bade kshetra marwar main jodhpur sambhag ke 6 jile-barmer, jaisalmer, jalaur, jodhpur, paali, sirohi kii kul 33 seat or nagaur jile kii 10 siton ko milakar kul 43 vidhansabha kshetra hai
 In the last election in Marwar, once a Congress bastion, the BJP demolished this stronghold by winning 39 seats
 congress ke khate main tatkaaleen mukhyamantri ashok gahalot kii seat samet mahaj teen seat ai jabaki ek seat par nirdaleey ne kabja jamaaya
 Jalore's five assembly seats - Ahor, Jalore, Bhinmal, Sanchore and Raniwara - are all occupied by BJP except Sanchore
 aahor vidhansabha kshetra sankhya 141 kii baat karen to yah saamaanya seat he
 According to the 2011 census, the population here is 303230, of which 94
 44 pratishat hissaa gramin or 5
 56 percent is urban
 vahiin kul aabaadi kaa 22
 03 per cent Scheduled Castes and 12
 39 fisadi anusuchit janajati hai
 62 in this seat in the 2013 assembly elections
 31 fisadi matdaan hua tha
 54 in the 2014 Lok Sabha elections
 97 fisadi matdaan hua tha
 Result of 2013 Assembly Election: In the 2013 Assembly Election, Shankar Singh Rajpurohit of BJP defeated Congress's Saivaram Patel by 9152 votes
 bijepi ke shankar singh raajpurohit ko 57808 or congress ke savaaram patel ko 48656 vot mili thea
 Result of 2008 Assembly Elections: In the 2008 assembly elections, former Congress MLA Bagh Raj Chaudhary defeated Chiranji Lal of BJP by 13751 votes
 vahiin 11553 voton ke saath nirdaleey ummidavaar ganpat singh tisare sthaan par rahen
 Congress' tiger Raj Chaudhary got 36253 votes and bjp's Chiranji Lal got 22502 votes

 bollywood ke superstar salmaan khan film 'bharat' ko box offis relies hue 10 din ho gaye hai
 However, the film's earnings have started declining now
 diarector ali abbaas jafar kii banaai 'bharat' ne apni relies ke 10wein din kareeb 5 karod kii kamai kii he, jo baaki dinon ke hisaab se kam he
 It is estimated that the Salman Khan and Katrina Kaif starrer has earned around 185 crores in 10 days
 film 'bharat' abhi tak 200 karod rupee kaa aankada nahin chhu saki he
 India 179 in its first week
 60 karod rupee kii kamai kii thi
 After this, the film did not do very well in the second week
 mana ja rahaa he ki taapasi pannu kii film game over kaa kuch asar bharat kii kamai par pad saktaa he
 If India did not earn 200 crores this week, then it will be a little difficult to stand in front of Shahid Kapoor's film Kabir Singh next week

 officiala post shared bysalman Khan (@beingsalmankhan) onmay 11, 2019 at 2:46 am PDT Let us know that Salman Khan and Katrina Kaif are still promoting their film India
 haal hi main salmaan ne apane bujurg phens ke liye is film kii khaas screening rakhi thi
 Salman Khan's film is being liked by fans of all his classes
 film bharat ek vyakti or desh kii kahani he, jisamen salmaan khan ko 5 alag-alag luks main dekh sakate hai
 The film also stars Disha Patni, Jackie Shroff, Tabu and Sunil Grover
 suraksha balon ne jammu-kashmir main sakriy aatankiyon kii hit list jari kii he jo ki unke nishane par hai
 The army believes that if it annihilates these top commanders, the backbone of terrorist organizations will be broken
 lihaaja kisi bhi surat main inkaa safaya karnaa suraksha balon kii praathamikta suchi main he
 The security forces have issued a list of 12 such terrorists active in Kashmir, who are no longer well
 philhal jammu-kashmir main hijbul mujahidin, lashkare taiyyaba or jaish e mohammad ke aatanki sakriy hai jinaki taadaad kareeb 200 he
 The first number among these terrorists is that of Abu Doojana of Lashkar Tayyiba
 pakistan kaa rahane vaala yah khoonkhaar aatanki lashkare taiyyaba kaa south kashmir kaa diviginal commander he
 It is an a ++ category terrorist who has a reward of about 15 lakhs on his head
 yah kai baar surakshabalon ko chakma dekar bhaag chukaa he
 It is too fast to escape and immediately changes its strategy and leaves the security forces
 kashmir main yah 2014 se sakriy he
 At number two is the name of Hijbul Mujahideen's Riyaz Naiko aka Zubair
 avantipura kaa rahane vaala yah aatanki philhal hijb pulavama main distric commander he
 It is also an a ++ category terrorist
 yah 2012 main aatanki bana tha
 Now that Hizbul's commander Sabzar has been killed, the possibility is that he will get the command of Hizbul
 agar hijbul kii kaman niko ko nahin milti he to isaki kaman saddaam paddar urf jaid ko mil sakati he
 He is currently the commander of Shopian of Hizbul Mujahideen
 yah bhi e++ category kaa aatanki he
 It is a close companion of Burhan Wani, a Hizbul-killed terrorist last year
 yah do saal pehle aatanki bana he lekin ilaake main isaki kaaphi dehshat he
 Abu Hamas is a terrorist of jaish-e-mohammed who hails from Pakistan
 yah san 2016 main jaish main bhartee hua
 He is the Divisional Commander of Jaish
 yah e++ category kaa kaaphi khoonkhaar aatanki mana jaataa he
 Hizbul Mujahideen divisional commander Zakir Rashid Bhatt alias Musa is also no less afraid
 musa ne haal hi main hurriyat conference ke netaaon ke sar kaatane kii dhamkee di thi
 Musa is an a ++ category terrorist active in Hizbul since 2013
 san 2013 main aatanki bana musa south kashmir ke avantipura kaa hi rahane vaala he or philhal hijbul se naaraaz chal rahaa he
 According to the security forces, not only that, lashkar-e-taiba district commander Shaukat Ahmed Talk aka Huzaifa is no less dangerous
 yah avantipura ke panjagam kaa rahane vaala he
 It is also an a ++ category terrorist who has been active since 2011
 lashkare taiyyaba kaa hi bashir ahamed vaani urf lashkar anantnag kaa distric commander he jo e++ category kaa aatanki he
 The militant hailing from Kokernag has been active since 2015
 lashkar kaa hi vaasim ahamed urf osama shopiyaan kaa eliti commander he
 This living also belongs to Shopian and has been a terrorist since 2014
 e++ category kaa yah khoonkhaar aatanki burhan vaani ke group main tha
 The dreaded terrorists Riyaz Naiko, Saddam Paddar, Shaukat Ahmed Talk, Wasim Ahmed, Zakir Rashid Bhatt and Zeenat ul Islam active in the Kashmir Valley
 hijbul mujahidin kaa altaaf ahamed daar urf kachuru bhi e++ category kaa aatanki he
 He is the district commander of Hizbul of Kulgam area
 yah san 2006 se sakriy he
 Hizbul Mujahideen's Budgam District Commander Mohammad Yasin Ittu alias Mansoor is a category terrorist
 2015 main aatanki bana ittu badgam ke hi chaddura kaa rahane vaala he
 Zeenat ul Islam alias Alkama is a lashkar-e-toiba terrorist who hails from Saugam Janipura in Shopian
 yah 2015 se lashkar kaa aatanki he
 Junaid Ahmed Mattoo alias Kandru is the district commander of lashkar-e-toiba
 kulgaam kaa rahane vaale canderu 2015 main aatanki bana he or e category kaa aatanki he
 It is generally believed that a terrorist does not remain active for more than seven years
 aatanki banane ke baad burhan vaani paanch saal ke bheetar maaraa gaya to sabjar chah saal main
 Not only this, Faizan was killed along with Sabzar within six months of becoming a terrorist
 tippaniyan Last year, 141 terrorists were killed in Jammu and Kashmir by security forces, while 56 terrorists have been killed so far this year
 abhi kashmir main 200 se 225 aatanki sakriy hai
 Of these, 100 to 125 are active in South Kashmir and the rest in North Kashmir
 south kashmir main surakshabalon ko oparation karne main isiilie dikkat aa rahi he
 Most of these terrorists are local
 local hone kii vajah se inkaa saport base bhi kaaphi he jiskaa phayda uthaakar yah aatanki bhaag jate hai
 At the same time, there are more number of foreign terrorists in North Kashmir
 vaise surakshabalon kii maane to ab jammu ilaake main aatanki na ke baraabar rah gaye hai
 Especially in places like Rajouri, Poonch, there are counting terrorists and they have little support from the local people
 surakshabalon kaa maananaa he ki jin aatankiyon kii tasviir jari ho chuki he ve to vaise bhi nishane par hai
 There are constant news about them
 aaj nahin to kal in saare khoonkhaar aatankiyon kaa safaya tay he

 19 se 21 ghante ke liye railyatri se 90 rupee charge kiye jaaenge
 100 passengers will be charged from the train for 22 to 24 hours
 48 ghante ke liye railyatri se 200 rupee charge kiye jaaenge
 This facility will increase the income of the railways, according to railway officials, by the fast booking of railway retiring rooms, while more and more passengers will be able to take advantage of it, on the other hand, the ease of booking the rest room for less time also reduces the burden on the pocket of people

 The Indian National Flag was adopted in its present form during a meeting of the Indian Constituent Assembly held on 22 July 1947, a few days before India's independence from the British on 15 August 1947
 ise 15 agast 1947 or 26 janvari 1950 ke bich bharat ke rashtriya dhvaj ke rup main apanaaya gaya

 3

 The highest flag of the country at a height of 493 meters is also hoisted in Ranchi itself
 4
 There is a law in the country called 'flag Code of India' (indian Flag Code), which sets the rules for hoisting the tricolor
 in niyamon kaa ulanghan karne waalon ko jail bhi ho sakati he

 tirangaa hameshaa coton, silk yaa phir khaadi kaa hi hona chahie

 6
